        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(accept4) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_accept4 found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_accept4)
                #error "__builtin_accept4 not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(accept4)
            __builtin_accept4;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

Working directory:  /Users/runner/work/Rayforge-iOS-ipa/Rayforge-iOS-ipa/glib-build/meson-private/tmp0678hiy8
Code:

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(fallocate) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_fallocate found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_fallocate)
                #error "__builtin_fallocate not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(fallocate)
            __builtin_fallocate;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }
-----------

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */

            #error "No definition for __builtin_getmntent_r found in the prefix"
        #endif

                #error "__builtin_getmntent_r not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(getmntent_r)
            __builtin_getmntent_r;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(memalign) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_memalign found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_memalign)
                #error "__builtin_memalign not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(memalign)
            __builtin_memalign;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }
-----------

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(prlimit) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_prlimit found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_prlimit)
                #error "__builtin_prlimit not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(prlimit)
            __builtin_prlimit;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(splice) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_splice found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_splice)
                #error "__builtin_splice not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(splice)
            __builtin_splice;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

#include <stdio.h>
int r;
int glib_underscore_test (void) { return 42; }
int main (int argc, char ** argv) {
  void *f1 = (void*)0, *f2 = (void*)0, *handle;
  handle = dlopen ((void*)0, 0);
  if (handle) {
    f1 = dlsym (handle, "glib_underscore_test");
    f2 = dlsym (handle, "_glib_underscore_test");

typedef struct fd_set {
 __int32_t fds_bits[((((1024) % ((sizeof(__int32_t) * 8))) == 0) ? ((1024) / ((sizeof(__int32_t) * 8))) : (((1024) / ((sizeof(__int32_t) * 8))) + 1))];
} fd_set;
int __darwin_check_fd_set_overflow(int, const void *, int) __attribute__((availability(macos,introduced=11.0))) __attribute__((availability(ios,introduced=14.0))) __attribute__((availability(tvos,introduced=14.0))) __attribute__((availability(watchos,introduced=7.0)));
inline __attribute__ ((__always_inline__)) int
__darwin_check_fd_set(int _a, const void *_b)
{
#pragma clang diagnostic push
#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wunguarded-availability-new"
 if ((uintptr_t)&__darwin_check_fd_set_overflow != (uintptr_t) 0) {
  return __darwin_check_fd_set_overflow(_a, _b, 0);
 } else {
  return 1;
 }
#pragma clang diagnostic pop
}
inline __attribute__ ((__always_inline__)) int
__darwin_fd_isset(int _fd, const struct fd_set *_p)
{
 if (__darwin_check_fd_set(_fd, (const void *) _p)) {
  return _p->fds_bits[(unsigned long)_fd / (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)] & ((__int32_t)(((unsigned long)1) << ((unsigned long)_fd % (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8))));
 }
 return 0;
}
inline __attribute__ ((__always_inline__)) void
__darwin_fd_set(int _fd, struct fd_set *const _p)
{
 if (__darwin_check_fd_set(_fd, (const void *) _p)) {
  (_p->fds_bits[(unsigned long)_fd / (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)] |= ((__int32_t)(((unsigned long)1) << ((unsigned long)_fd % (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)))));
 }
}
inline __attribute__ ((__always_inline__)) void
__darwin_fd_clr(int _fd, struct fd_set *const _p)
{
 if (__darwin_check_fd_set(_fd, (const void *) _p)) {
  (_p->fds_bits[(unsigned long)_fd / (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)] &= ~((__int32_t)(((unsigned long)1) << ((unsigned long)_fd % (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)))));
 }
}

__darwin_check_fd_set(int _a, const void *_b)

#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wunguarded-availability-new"

inline __attribute__ ((__always_inline__)) int
__darwin_fd_isset(int _fd, const struct fd_set *_p)
{

  return _p->fds_bits[(unsigned long)_fd / (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)] & ((__int32_t)(((unsigned long)1) << ((unsigned long)_fd % (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8))));
 }
 return 0;
}

__darwin_fd_set(int _fd, struct fd_set *const _p)

  (_p->fds_bits[(unsigned long)_fd / (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)] |= ((__int32_t)(((unsigned long)1) << ((unsigned long)_fd % (sizeof(__int32_t) * 8)))));

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(reallocarray) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_reallocarray found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_reallocarray)
                #error "__builtin_reallocarray not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(reallocarray)
            __builtin_reallocarray;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }
